## [Aug 28 - Sep 03, 2023](/content/2023/35/README.md)

### Software / Communication - Video Conferencing

([Demo](https://rsshub.app), [Source Code (‚≠ê26k)](https://github.com/DIYgod/RSSHub)) `MIT` `Nodejs/Docker`

### Software / Miscellaneous

*   [Watcharr (‚≠ê8)](https://github.com/sbondCo/Watcharr) - A free and open source content watch list. Add and track all the shows and movies you are watching. Comes with user authentication, modern and clean UI and a very simple setup. ([Demo](https://beta.watcharr.app/)) `MIT` `Docker`
